## Analysis

### Recommendations

1. Remove or conditionally execute code using Node.js globals
2. Ensure middleware.ts and auth.config.ts have no module-level side effects
3. Add explicit `export const runtime = "edge"` declarations
4. Use Edge Runtime-compatible alternatives where needed
